2._CD ``_``

4._CD ``_``
There_EX is_VBZ no_DT necessary_JJ for_IN me_PRP to_TO say_VB much_RB as_IN to_TO the_DT rationale_NN of_IN the_DT treatment_NN ._.
Surgeon_NNP Hall_NNP R._NNP A._NN ,_, the_DT originator_NN ,_, has_VBZ made_VBN it_PRP public_JJ ._.
Chloral_JJ Hydrate_NNP being_VBG a_DT powerful_JJ sedative_JJ soothes_NNS the_DT irritated_JJ nerves_NNS ,_, and_CC so_RB relaxes_VB the_DT contracted_JJ vessels_NNS ,_, the_DT blood_NN is_VBZ once_RB more_JJR uniformly_JJ distributed_VBN and_CC consequently_RB the_DT pulse_JJ re-appears_NNS at_IN the_DT wrist_NN ,_, the_DT cramps_NNS and_CC burning_VBG abdominal_JJ pains_NNS subside_RB ,_, sleep_NN is_VBZ induced_VBN ,_, the_DT respiration_NN be-_NN comes_VBZ regular_JJ ,_, the_DT discharges_NNS lessen_VBP ,_, the_DT face_NN fills_VBZ out_RP ,_, the_DT voice_NN becomes_VBZ stronger_JJR and_CC the_DT natural_JJ secretions_NNS are_VBP restored._JJ ``_``
